# AI Study Guide

## Introduction

Artificial Intelligence is transforming the world.

## Machine Learning

Machine learning enables systems to learn patterns from data.

## Deep Learning

Deep learning uses neural networks with multiple layers.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

# AI Study Guide

## Introduction

Artificial Intelligence is transforming the world.

## Machine Learning

Machine learning enables systems to learn patterns from data.

## Deep Learning

Deep learning uses neural networks with multiple layers.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

# AI Study Guide

## Introduction

Artificial Intelligence is transforming the world.

## Machine Learning

Machine learning enables systems to learn patterns from data.

## Deep Learning

Deep learning uses neural networks with multiple layers.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

# AI Study Guide

## Introduction

Artificial Intelligence is transforming the world.

## Machine Learning

Machine learning enables systems to learn patterns from data.

## Deep Learning

Deep learning uses neural networks with multiple layers.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

# AI Study Guide

## Introduction

Artificial Intelligence is transforming the world.

## Machine Learning

Machine learning enables systems to learn patterns from data.

## Deep Learning

Deep learning uses neural networks with multiple layers.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

# AI Study Guide

## Introduction

Artificial Intelligence is transforming the world.

## Machine Learning

Machine learning enables systems to learn patterns from data.

## Deep Learning

Deep learning uses neural networks with multiple layers.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

# AI Study Guide

## Introduction

Artificial Intelligence is transforming the world.

## Machine Learning

Machine learning enables systems to learn patterns from data.

## Deep Learning

Deep learning uses neural networks with multiple layers.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

# AI Study Guide

## Introduction

Artificial Intelligence is transforming the world.

## Machine Learning

Machine learning enables systems to learn patterns from data.

## Deep Learning

Deep learning uses neural networks with multiple layers.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

# AI Study Guide

## Introduction

Artificial Intelligence is transforming the world.

## Machine Learning

Machine learning enables systems to learn patterns from data.

## Deep Learning

Deep learning uses neural networks with multiple layers.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.

# AI Study Guide

## Introduction

Artificial Intelligence is transforming the world.

## Machine Learning

Machine learning enables systems to learn patterns from data.

## Deep Learning

Deep learning uses neural networks with multiple layers.

## RAG Systems

RAG combines retrieval and generation for better AI responses.

## Applications

-   Chatbots
-   Recommendation systems
-   Image recognition
-   Search engines

## Key Concepts

-   Embeddings
-   Vector databases
-   Transformers
-   Attention mechanism

## Example Code

``` python
print("RAG system working")
```

## Conclusion

AI systems are rapidly evolving and shaping the future.
